name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Cozy Queen Room
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Couples
info:1 Review
rating:5
posted:Posted May 16, 2024
msg:We stayed at the Qinman hotel 13-16.05.24 for the trip to Huangshan mountain and nearby Hongcu village. Despite the hotel situated ~3km from the tourist bus stop we find the location one of the big benefits: there is no hustle, loud noises of the cars and hordes of tourists: you can peacefully relax and enjoy quite and slow mornings and evenings. The hotel is beautifully designed? Rooms are spacious and perfectly cleaned. The staff of the hotel is very attentive to all questions, very friendly and polite, even despite we didn't speak Chinese the personal organized our stay perfectly and used WeChat with translations to give online feedback to any requests! Special thanks to Ms. 慧慧 HuiHui she helped organize transfers, morning breakfast for takeaway and tea with delights to our hot springs. Worth to note! This hotel has its own private hot springs, in May temperature in n the evening can go down to ~18C, fresh hot water helps you relax after long busy days and mind can fully rest in the silence of the night. One of the surprises of the stay was free laundry, it is extremely useful after hikes in n the mountains. Hotel restaurant has great breakfast with local farmer's products and freshly ground good coffee from reputable roasters. If you are a tea lover you'll find tea store from farmers just in front of the main gates, in the rooms you'll find local tea and tea set for tea ceremonies 😀. What is more? The dinner is delicious, especially local fishes. If you arrive by the bus to Tangkou the hotel staff can organize a transfer from and to bus station for free. We highly recommend Qinman hotel for everyone!

name:S‍t‍e‍v‍e‍n
info:Cozy Queen Room
info:Stayed in December 2022
info:Friends
info:5 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted December 26, 2022
msg:I have just returned from a three day stay at Huangshan Qinman Resort Hotel and enjoyed every moment. The room was spaceous and spotlessly clean with a huge circular bathtub as well as an excellent rain shower. We were given a warm welcome on arrival and check in was super quick. 
As it was -2--4 outside the AC and underfloor heating made the room comfortable in minutes as we settled in to enjoy some tea and welcome snacks.
Breakfast was served in our room and arrived looking like a banquet fit for a king! Very many small dishes rangine from Sweet Potato, egg, cakes, noodles, shu mei and Baozi. Definitely enough to set you up for a days hiking on Yellow Mountain.  
The staff were very helpful in pointing out where we should go on the mountain and what was best to see.  They also provided us with a car ride to catch the bus to the cablecar and also to and from the main town at night so we could have dinner out. On returning each night we were presented with a traditional dessert and some fruits.
Huangshan Qinman Resort Hotel also has hot springs and we made use of these each night. After a few minutes to get used to the spring we would be greeted with Tea and some light snacks which was wonderful.
As we checked out shortly after breakfast on the last morning we were presented with some gift boxes of local cakes. A lovely guesture.

I can highly recommend this Hotel to anyone visiting the area.  I was made to feel so welcome and would happily stay here again next time I visit Huangshan.

The hotel's housekeeper contacted us a week in advance and asked if there was anything we needed to prepare in advance, which was very good. On the day we were going to Huangshan, the housekeeper Huihui asked us about our arrival time early in the morning. When we arrived at the hotel, she helped us with our luggage and introduced the hotel to us. At first, I didn't notice that the room had a private hot spring. When I saw the room, my family was very satisfied. Everyone took a hot spring bath during the nights we stayed, especially after climbing Huangshan. It was very refreshing. The hotel's housekeeper was also very nice. On the first day, when she saw that we didn't eat breakfast in time, she sent a message to ask if we needed it delivered to the room. She also reminded us to tell them before taking a hot spring bath. Then, every time, the aunt in charge of cleaning would come to help clean the pool and then help drain the water. After confirming the time to climb Huangshan with us, she would remind us not to buy raincoats and hiking poles, as the hotel would provide them. During the May Day holiday, the hotel happened to have a Huizhou paper-cutting experience parent-child study activity. The lady at the front desk also called and sent a message to invite us to participate. The invited study teacher was very professional and kind. On the day of departure, the hotel also gave us Huangshan specialty sesame cakes as souvenirs. In general, it is a very warm homestay hotel with a very good environment and considerate service.

name:G‍u‍e‍s‍t‍ ‍U‍s‍e‍r
info:Cozy Queen Room
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:7 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 11, 2024
msg:The hotel housekeeper sent us photos and videos in advance, but when we saw the parking lot sign of Qinman Resort Hotel, we still didn't know how to get there. Fortunately, the hotel housekeeper came to the front of the car to lead us. It turned out that we drove up from the corridor between the two buildings. In fact, if the hotel can buy the wall advertising space near the corridor of the two buildings and make a sign, it should be much easier to find. The mess of these two buildings, corridors and parking lots made our first impression very bad. But entering the hotel area immediately makes people's eyes bright, and the overall cleanliness is very tidy. There are large areas of green plants in the courtyard, and there are outdoor hot springs. The hotel housekeeper has been leading the way. Because it was drizzling, the housekeeper also held an umbrella for us. There are also snacks for check-in. Entering the room, I smelled some moldy smells. Maybe Huangshan is still too humid, but it will be fine if I open the window for ventilation for a while. In fact, the hotel can do better. Either the housekeeper opens the window for ventilation in advance, or turns on the air conditioner every day to remove moisture. Fortunately, the quilt on the bed is very dry, there is no feeling of moisture, and it is very comfortable. There is a road in front of the room window, which is a little noisy, but there is a mountain across the road. It is really open to the window and see the mountain, full of green. The decoration is simple and generous, with just the right sense of technology. The curtains are electric, the lights are divided into 4 modes, and the mirror in the washroom has lights and defogger functions. There are snacks and tea sets on the coffee table in front of the window. The snacks are delicious and we ate them all. In short, there are some small shortcomings here, but you can feel the hotel's intentions everywhere. I guess it is a young team. I can feel that the whole team wants to do a good job of the hotel. For this effort, I also want to give them 5 stars. Of course, if the shortcomings can be improved, it will be better. The hotel housekeeper also asked kindly whether we needed laundry and hot springs. Because the weather was cold, we were worried that we would catch a cold in the outdoor hot springs, so we gave up the hot springs. By the way, the hotel housekeeper Huihui's service throughout the whole process was very considerate. Since there were not many guests staying in the hotel, the breakfast on the second day was provided according to the single set meal. There were fewer varieties, but it was enough to eat, and the Cantonese dim sum tasted really good.

msg:The room is in a modern minimalist style and is equipped with a projector. It is very comfortable to watch movies while lying on the bed. The service is attentive. You can order food through WeChat and go straight to the restaurant to save time and efficiency. After getting off the high-speed rail, you can take a bus from the high-speed rail station (the journey takes about 45 minutes) to the transfer center. Contact the hotel to send a car to the hotel. It is a 5-minute drive from the transfer center to the hotel. If you go to Huangshan, you have to go to this transfer center. The hotel's breakfast is a set meal, with six snacks (shrimp dumplings, steamed dumplings, siomai, etc.), whole-grain eggs, noodles or wonton stew, and a buffet of milk, soy milk, and fruit. It's a good combination. This winter trip to Huangshan Mountain splits the peaks. There is no need to queue up whether you take the scenic bus or the cable car. Due to the weather, you can’t go up the mountain on a rainy day because it rained the day before. When the sun comes up, you can see the indescribable sea of ​​clouds in Huangshan Mountain. OK. Perfect.

msg:Summary: low cost performance, advised to give up.
Don't come if you are looking for hot springs. The main hot spring is really average. The hot spring water is very dirty, with a layer of floating ash and dead mosquitoes floating on it.
Don't come if you're looking for a swimming pool. The open-air swimming pool is not constant temperature, but has cold water. You can't go into the water in winter. There is also a layer of garbage floating on the surface of the swimming pool.
The room is facing the road and the noise is very loud. Because it was boring to turn on the air conditioner, I opened the window. It was too noisy, so I had no choice but to turn off the air conditioner and sleep with the window closed.
The hotel room is quite large, but if you don't want to use the hot spring, the price of this room is 800+, which is not worth it. Dissuade me from quitting, the price/performance ratio is not high.

            "Climbing Huangshan Mountain without Climbing the Five Sacred Mountains"
                       Jin Chanzi
Climb the Yellow Mountains before climbing the Five Mountains. The mountains are high and the clouds stop around the pine rocks.
Cloud gauze covers the body and suddenly the peak appears, the majestic god and the king of the palace are angry.
Walking on the infinite ladder with a stick, the endless mountain scenery changes with every step.
Travelers climb around Lotus Peak and accidentally enter the clouds to cultivate immortality.

With weak legs, I descended vertically from the peak, and climbed down Huangshan Mountain with my eyes closed.
The poets check in to welcome guests, and the lone monkey observes all living beings in the sea.
Huangshan tea is brewed in Huangshan water, and outsiders climb Huangshan rocks.
The stream lies in the west and south of the river, with winding paths and green fields.

msg:Qinman, this name is as gentle as her beautiful boss. This is the second trip to Huangshan after 12 years. Because I chose Qinman, I added a lot of warm and beautiful feelings.
The moment the car drove to the door, um, the dangling heart finally let go, and I felt that I liked it. Sure enough, after entering, I looked up and saw the large cascading stone wall, wow! surprise! The design of the yard is also very stylish, and you can see all kinds of cute little plants everywhere (there is also a tree with pink flowers on the second floor, it is very beautiful, I don’t know what it is called. Well, that large quaint stone wall is in these gentle plants Against the background, let my heart ripple wave after wave of moved.
On the other side of the yard is a rectangular open-air swimming pool, an artifact to cool off the heat.
After checking in in the lobby on the second floor, the gentle lady took us to the room. It is full of coolness (the air conditioner is turned on in advance), and there are no redundant and complicated decorations. The large room is simple and high-grade in black, white, gray and log colors. The black thin-mouthed ceramic electric kettle is equipped with a ceramic tray and a cat's paw glass. There are two bottles of Evian mineral water next to it, and two bottles of Thai elephant soda in the small refrigerator in the cabinet below. Local specialty snacks are also prepared on the coffee table. The two-meter wide bed is clean, soft and comfortable. The bathroom is my personal favorite. It truly separates wet and dry. The TOTO smart toilet is separated from the shower area next to it. The large washbasin, double washbasins, and gold-copper KOHLER faucet have a sense of luxury. What surprises me here is that the toiletries are LE LABO, and the elegant fragrance of bergamot is relaxing (I like it very much, and the amount is very sufficient. In the spirit of environmental protection, it is mainly easy to use. Hey, I also took it to the hotel on the mountain later. ).
Well, in addition to the swimming pool, there are also billiards tables, treadmills, etc. The place is not very big, but the grandfathers at the back go down and play billiards and have a lot of fun. There is also a small bar next to it. Upstairs, the grass on the rooftop should also be able to set up a tent and have a picnic, barbecue or something. Oh, by the way, there are several hot spring pools on the rooftop upstairs. After climbing the mountain, the hot springs will definitely relieve fatigue, especially Huangshan. I still remember the sore legs that year.
We ate dinner at the hotel. The restaurant is very spacious and clean. We ordered braised chicken, scrambled eggs with shi'er (shi'er is a local specialty, please Baidu haha), and fresh bamboo shoots and roasted meat. It's delicious, real The taste of the farmhouse, the three of them had enough to eat, and finally gave us a large plate of watermelon, but we couldn't eat it anymore. Seeing that it was very fresh, one of us took a small piece and tasted it. It's not bad.
In the evening, there are small sweet soups such as mung bean soup, if needed, the aunt will deliver it to the room. Anyway, it's a little warmth.
Well, I accidentally discovered that the room was named after a solar term. My curiosity drove me to take a sneak peek at the door of every room on the same floor, and found that it was named after a solar term. Later, I learned from the boss that the hotel has a total of 24 rooms, and all of them are named after the 24 solar terms. I am creative and like it.
The boss is very young, gentle and delicate in appearance, demure and elegant, and even a little shy haha, he is the type I like. (At first, I didn't expect it to be the boss. I always thought it was the hotel manager. I didn't know until I made a reservation after going down the mountain. It made an oolong hehe)
In a word, this hotel is spacious, bright, comfortable, a**ospheric, and has no commercial a**osphere. From the boss to the little brothers, sisters and aunts, they get along very naturally. I have a sense of healing here.
I, who almost never write reviews, would like to use this article "'Small Composition'" to express my love and gratitude to Qinman and the "Qinman people". (After going down the mountain, I broke the original plan and renewed for one night, and the room discount was upgraded. Even better, it comes with a large round bathtub, but unfortunately the video I shot can't be put here, it should be seen by other users' comments)
Attached is no PS and no sequence photos, the level is limited but real.

msg:強烈推薦這家酒店，全屋智能極簡設計，房間設施新，床品舒服，服務人員素質高，來黃山，旅行中的驚喜，美好的回憶，（去黃山來她家你不需要帶腦子）真的是為黃山之行加分.景上添花
1當天大連出發 管家蕾蕾和香香就會電話溝通，確認一下我們的到達時間，加微信，告訴我們停車場位置，以及一些疑問都會耐心解答（貼心服務）
2去黃山的會免費接送 為我們接送換乘車站。（1vs1服務）【因為我們是租車來這裏，把車停她家停車場，安心旅行就可】
3黃山的雨衣和枴杖都為你提供好免費贈送。（去黃山一切為你準備到位）
4晚上我們來的較晚，會給你準備夜宵（銀耳羹）加分了
5早餐：可以去一樓吃，也可給送上門。（我們選擇送車門）超級貼心，早餐很豐富level很高。有圖展示 又加分
6香香和蕾蕾會給送到屋內。介紹冰箱內的東西可無償使用。依雲和大象氣泡水。還有一些飲料和點心。逼格烘託起來了
7洗手盆和龍頭科勒，馬桶toto。沐浴洗漱品歐舒丹。全屋智能。

確定沒想到黃山下有那麼好的酒店，夜景超級美，燈光3000k暖光特別有層次感，氛圍烘託，很高級。（一猜就是年輕的老闆）
8有健身房和桌球廳，夏天還有游泳池，對於愛運動的小夥伴一定會加分。如果夏天一定很難預訂！一屋難求。
9臨走的時候還為我們送上伴手禮…
太走心了，絕對是網紅打卡店了，相信我來黃山去他家，一定會帶給你不一樣的體驗！

msg:真的是很用心的酒店。從山上下來南門2公里就到，特別方便，管家式服務非常貼心。謝謝香香的接待。
身心俱疲的時候酒店還主動提出幫忙洗衣烘衣，3小時不到就疊好送回房間了！神奇！感動！
全套lelabo的洗護套裝，小冰箱贈飲免費還有多款迎賓點心，酒店整體設施和硬件也很新。房間很寬敞温馨。
晚上管家香香還主動提出要出車送我們去做核酸，推辭了自己去，後來發覺還是有必要的…地方在一個停車場三樓，容易開錯口繞圈。
小建議：
1. 早飯定食的品種和數量有點太多了，應該很少有人每樣都合胃口，可以簡單地讓客人自選幾樣，以免浪費。
2. 房間窗簾遮光性不好，早上很亮。晚上洗漱台的智能鏡子又亮着燈關不掉、也沒有門，房間裏光污染影響睡眠。
